CREATE TABLE colis (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    dateEnregistrement DATETIME NOT NULL,
    nomEmploye VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    prenomEmploye VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    numeroTalonMco VARCHAR(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    numeroLta VARCHAR(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    nomNatureProduit VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    poidsProduit DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    dateEnvoi DATE NOT NULL,
    dateEstimeeArrivee DATE NOT NULL,
    departArrivee VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    coutTransport DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    nomProprietaire VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    prenomProprietaire VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    numeroCnibPassport VARCHAR(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    numeroTelephone1 VARCHAR(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    numeroTelephone2 VARCHAR(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
    email VARCHAR(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
    statusColis ENUM('LIVRÉ', 'NON LIVRÉ') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
